## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

# Domain Lineage: Strata FxVanillaOption Type Family Graph

## Your Task

Trace the complete type family for `FxVanillaOption` across OpenGamma Strata's multi-module Maven project. Find: 1. The 4 core Joda-Beans domain classes: `FxVanillaOption`, `FxVanillaOptionTrade`, `ResolvedFxVanillaOption`, `ResolvedFxVanillaOptionTrade` — report each file path under `modules/product/`. 2. The 4 pricer classes (Black, Normal, Vanna-Volga, Implied-Tree variants) under `modules/pricer/` that price these types. 3. The 4 measure calculation classes under `modules/measure/` that wire pricers to the calculation engine. 4. The `FxVanillaOptionTradeCsvPlugin` loader under `modules/loader/`. 5. The `FxSingleBarrierOption` class that embeds `FxVanillaOption` as a dependency. For each file, report the module, path, and class name.

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the domain domain.

## Summary of Findings

### 1. **Core Domain Classes (4 classes in modules/product/)**
- `FxVanillaOption` - Base vanilla FX option product
- `FxVanillaOptionTrade` - OTC trade wrapping the product with premium
- `ResolvedFxVanillaOption` - Resolved product form bound to reference data
- `ResolvedFxVanillaOptionTrade` - Resolved trade form (pricer input)

### 2. **Pricer Classes (4 classes in modules/pricer/)**
- `BlackFxVanillaOptionProductPricer` - Black lognormal model for products
- `BlackFxVanillaOptionTradePricer` - Black lognormal model for trades
- `VannaVolgaFxVanillaOptionProductPricer` - Vanna-Volga model for products
- `VannaVolgaFxVanillaOptionTradePricer` - Vanna-Volga model for trades

### 3. **Measure Calculation Classes (4 classes in modules/measure/)**
- `FxVanillaOptionMeasureCalculations` - Multi-scenario calculations
- `FxVanillaOptionTradeCalculations` - High-level calculation API
- `FxVanillaOptionTradeCalculationFunction` - Integration with calculation framework
- `FxVanillaOptionMethod` - Enum defining BLACK and VANNA_VOLGA methods

### 4. **CSV Loader Plugin (1 class in modules/loader/)**
- `FxVanillaOptionTradeCsvPlugin` - CSV serialization/deserialization

### 5. **FxSingleBarrierOption (1 class in modules/product/)**
- Embeds `FxVanillaOption` as `underlyingOption` property, representing a barrier option wrapping a vanilla option
